# <a name="office-365-education"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-105">Office 365 教育版</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-105">Office 365 Education</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-106">Microsoft Office 365 提供各種可滿足貴組織需求的最佳計劃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-106">Microsoft Office 365 is available in a variety of plans to best meet the needs of your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-107">如果您想要知道 Office 365 教育版方案有何差異，本文將說明各方案中包含的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-107">If you're looking for the differences between the Office 365 plans, including Exchange Online plans, this article will show you which features are included in each of them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-108">Office 365 與知名的 Microsoft Office 桌面套件結合，搭載 Microsoft 新一代通訊與共同作業服務的雲端架構版本 (包括 Microsoft Exchange Online、Microsoft SharePoint Online、Office 網頁版，以及 Microsoft 商務用 Skype Online)，讓使用者可透過網際網路在任何地點執行工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-108">Office 365 combines the familiar Microsoft Office desktop suite with cloud-based versions of Microsoft's next-generation communications and collaboration services—including Microsoft Exchange Online, Microsoft SharePoint Online, Office Online, and Microsoft Skype for Business Online—to help users be productive from virtually anywhere through the Internet.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-109">本文列出適用於 Office 365 教育版方案 (A1、A3 和 A5) 的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-109">This article lists the features for Office 365 education plans (A1, A3, and A5).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-110">若要跨商務和企業方案比較功能，請參閱[比較商務用 Office 365 方案](https://www.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/business/compare-more-office-365-for-business-plans)，或如需更詳細的功能清單，請參閱相關的服務描述：[Office 365 服務說明](../office-365-service-descriptions-technet-library.md) (部分內容機器翻譯)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-110">To compare features across plans, see [Compare Office 365 for Business plans](https://www.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/business/compare-more-office-365-for-business-plans) or, for a more detailed list of features, see the relevant service description at [Office 365 Service Descriptions [TechNet Library]](../office-365-service-descriptions-technet-library.md).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-111">若要搜尋技術支援文章和資訊，請參閱 [Office 說明和訓練](https://support.office.com/) (部分內容機器翻譯)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-111">To search for support articles and information, see [Office Support](https://support.office.com/).</span></span>
  
## <a name="service-availability-for-each-plan"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-112">每個方案可用的服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-112">Service availability for each plan</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-113">每個 Office 365 教育方案皆包含一些個別服務，例如 Exchange Online 和 SharePoint Online。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-113">Each Office 365 plan includes a number of individual services, such as Exchange Online and SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-114">下表顯示每項 Office 365 方案中可用的服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-114">The following table shows the services that are available in each Office 365 plan.</span></span>

## <a name="office-365-security-amp-compliance-center-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-629">Office 365 安全性與合規性中心功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-629">Office 365 Security &amp; Compliance Center</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-630">[Office 365 安全性與合規性中心](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/compliance/go-to-the-securitycompliance-center)旨在協助您為貴組織的 Office 365 管理合規性功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-630">[] The [Office 365 Security &amp; Compliance Center](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/compliance/go-to-the-securitycompliance-center) is designed to help you manage compliance features across Office 365 for your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-631">現有 SharePoint 和 Exchange 合規性功能的連結可將整個 Office 365 的合規性功能結合在一起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-631">Links to existing SharePoint and Exchange compliance features bring together compliance capabilities across Office 365.</span></span> 
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p119">Currently, many of the compliance features are still accessible through service-specific management interfaces, such as the Exchange admin center (EAC). However, this will change in the future as more service-independent compliance features are added to the Security &amp; Compliance Center.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p119">Currently, many of the compliance features are still accessible through service-specific management interfaces, such as the Exchange admin center (EAC). However, this will change in the future as more service-independent compliance features are added to the Security &amp; Compliance Center.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-706"><sup>1</sup> 資料控管讓使用者建立、發佈並手動將標籤套用至文件；使用磁碟機寄送或透過網路匯入資料；以及在工作負載、使用者和群組之間建立與套用保留/刪除原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-706"><sup>1</sup> Data governance lets users create, publish, and manually apply labels to documents; import data using drive shipping or over the network; and create and apply retention/deletion policies across workloads, users, and groups.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-707">將保留原則套用到信箱需要 Office 365 企業版 E3 或 E5。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-707">Retention policies applied to mailboxes require Office 365 Enterprise E3 or E5.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-708"> 
<sup>2</sup> 進階資料控管可讓您保留重要的資訊，並根據保留或刪除原則或兩者，藉由分類資訊來刪除不重要的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-708"> 
<sup>2</sup> Advanced data governance allows you to retain important information and delete unimportant information by classifying information based on a retention or deletion policy or both.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-709">其中包括智慧型/自動化動作，例如建議原則；自動將標籤套用至資料；根據敏感性資料類型或查詢套用標籤；以及使用智慧匯入篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-709">It includes intelligent/automated actions such as recommending policies; automatically applying labels to data; applying labels based on sensitive data types or queries; and use of smart import filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-710">其中也包含監督功能，可讓您針對安全性與合規性目的檢閱員工通訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-710">It also includes the Supervision feature for reviewing employee communications for security and compliance purposes.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-711"> 
<sup>3</sup> 無限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-711"> 
<sup>3</sup> Unlimited.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-712"> 
<sup>4</sup> 美國及西歐 (荷蘭) 區域支援進階電子文件探索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-712"> 
<sup>4</sup> Advanced eDiscovery is supported in the United States and in the Western Europe (Netherlands) region.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-713">(來自加拿大和亞太地區的客戶資料會匯出至美國。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-713">(Customer data from Canada and Asia Pacific is exported to the United States.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-714">來自歐洲、中東和非洲的客戶資料會匯出到西歐 [荷蘭]。)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-714">Customer data from Europe, the Middle East, and Africa is exported to Western Europe [Netherlands].)</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-715"> 
<sup>5</sup> 進階威脅防護可在 Office 365 A5 中使用，可作為 Office 365 A1 和 Office 365 A3 的獨立服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-715">

## <a name="office-for-the-web-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-920">網頁版 Office 的功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-920">Office for the web Service Description</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-921">下表提供 Office 365 教育版方案中可用網頁版 Office 功能和具備豐富功能的 Microsoft Office 桌面應用程式比較的連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-921">The following table provides links to comparisons of Office for the web feature capabilities available in Office 365 education plans to feature-rich Microsoft Office desktop apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-922">使用此比較表了解網頁版 Office 提供的功能，然後選取功能名稱，即可閱讀該功能的簡短描述。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-922">Use the comparisons to discover what features are available in Office Online, and then click on the feature name to read a brief description about how that feature works.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-923">您會發現組織中有些人可能需要使用 Excel 桌面應用程式的進階圖表功能，然而，有些人只需要透過網頁版 Office 來檢視和局部編輯 Word 文件與 PowerPoint 簡報。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-923">You may discover that some people in your organization may need the advanced charting capability of the Excel desktop app while others may only need to view and lightly edit Word documents and PowerPoint presentations with Office Online.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-924">Office 桌面套件涵蓋了 Office 的有限精選功能，提供進階功能讓您運用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-924">A limited selection of Office features has been chosen to represent the advanced capabilities of the Office desktop suite.</span></span> <br/>
> - <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-925">此資料表未完整列出 Microsoft Office 的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-925">The comparison tables are not a comprehensive list of Microsoft Office features.</span></span> <br/> 
> - <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-926">Microsoft Office 365 專業增強版是最新版 Office 桌面套件推出的每月訂閱產品項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-926">Microsoft Office 365 ProPlus is a monthly subscription offer of the latest Office desktop suite.</span></span> <br/>
> - <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-927">如果 Microsoft Office Online Server 內部部署客戶已購買 Office 桌面套件授權 (例如：Office 專業增強版、Office 標準版或 Office 365 專業增強版授權)，則可取得網頁版 Office 的編輯授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-927">> Microsoft Office Web Apps Server 2013 on-premises customers get an Office Online editing license if they have purchased an Office desktop suite license (such as an Office Professional Plus, Office Standard, or Office 365 ProPlus license).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1361"><sup>1</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是內部部署伺服器，必須個別採購並管理，以便啟用支援的 IRM 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1361"><sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features.</span></span> <br/>
<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1362"><sup>2</sup> 傳輸規則由彈性準則構成，可讓您定義條件和例外狀況，以及根據準則採取的動作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1362">Transport rules are made up of flexible criteria, which allow you to define conditions and exceptions, and actions to take based on the criteria.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1363">MO_ExchangeOnline 和 Microsoft ExchangeServer2013 之間可用的準則和動作並不相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1363">The available criteria and actions differ between Exchange Online, and Microsoft Exchange Server 2013.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1364">如需可用準則和動作的清單，請參閱每一個產品對應的準則和動作主題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1364">For a list of available criteria and actions, see the corresponding criteria and actions topics for each product.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1365"> 
<sup>3</sup> Exchange Server 2013 僅使用 Microsoft 反惡意程式碼引擎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1365">Exchange Server 2013 uses only the Microsoft anti-malware engine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1366">Exchange Online 使用多個反惡意程式碼引擎，來掃描輸入、輸出和內部訊息中是否有惡意程式碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1366">Exchange Online uses multiple anti-malware engines to scan inbound, outbound, and internal messages for malware.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1367"> 
<sup>4</sup> SharePoint Online 必須包含在 Office 365 訂閱計劃中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1367">SharePoint Online must be included in the O365_W14_2nd subscription plan.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1368"> 
<sup>5</sup> 已連線的帳戶支援 POP 和 IMAP 帳戶，但對 Outlook.com (Hotmail) 停用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1368">Connected accounts are supported for POP & IMAP accounts, but disabled for Outlook.com (Hotmail).</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1369"><sup>6</sup> 不支援使用 Cmdlet 來使用通訊清單及全域通訊清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1369">Using a cmdlet to work with the Address List and Global Address List is not supported.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1370"> 
<sup>7</sup> 部分第三方 Web 組件和增益集可能無法使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1370">Some third-party web parts and add-ins may not be available.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1371"> 
<sup>8</sup> 對於電子文件探索，您需要為內部部署與雲端進行不同的查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1371">For eDiscovery, you need a separate query for on-premises vs. cloud.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1372"> 
<sup>9</sup> 資料表指出用戶端是否與相關的計劃搭配運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1372">Table indicates whether or not the client works with the associated plans.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1373">其並不代表這些計劃的採購中必須包含用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1373">It does not mean the clients are necessarily included in the purchase of these plans.</span></span> 
  
### <a name="exchange-online-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1374">Exchange Online 限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1374">Exchange Online limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1375">尋找不同服務區域的 Exchange Online 限制，包括通訊錄限制、信箱儲存限制以及報告與郵件追蹤限制，以上所列僅是其中幾例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1375">Find the Exchange Online limits for a variety of service areas, including address book limits, mailbox storage limits, and reporting and message trace limits, to name just a few.</span></span>

#### <a name="address-book-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1404">通訊錄限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1404">Address book limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p142">**通訊清單限制** 可以在 Exchange Online 或 Exchange Server 2013 組織中建立的通訊清單數目上限。這個數目包括 Exchange Online 中的預設通訊清單，例如 [所有連絡人] 和 [所有群組]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p142">**Address list limit** The maximum number of address lists that can be created in an Exchange Online or Exchange Server 2013 organization. This number includes the default address lists in Exchange Online, such as All Contacts and All Groups.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1407">**離線通訊錄限制** 可以在 Exchange Online 或 Exchange Server 2013 組織中建立的離線通訊錄 (OAB) 數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1407">**Offline address book limit** The maximum number of offline address books (OAB) that can be created in an Exchange Online or Exchange Server 2013 organization.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1408">**通訊錄原則限制** 可以在 Exchange Online 或 Exchange Server 2013 組織中建立的通訊錄原則 (ABP) 數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1408">**Address book policies limit** The maximum number of address book policies (ABP) that be created in an Exchange Online or Exchange Server 2013 organization.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1409">**全域通訊清單** 可以在 Exchange Online 或 Exchange Server 2013 組織中建立的全域通訊清單 (GAL) 數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1409">**Global address lists** The maximum number of global address lists (GAL) that be created in an Exchange Online or Exchange Server 2013 organization.</span></span>

#### <a name="mailbox-storage-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1430">信箱儲存限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1430">Mailbox storage limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p143">可用的信箱儲存容量取決於信箱類型和使用者的訂閱授權。管理員可降低單一使用者或全域的最高信箱大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p143">The amount of mailbox storage available is determined by the mailbox type and the user's subscription license. Administrators can reduce maximum mailbox sizes per user or globally.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p144">不允許使用日誌記錄、傳輸規則或自動轉寄規則將郵件複製到 Exchange Online 信箱以進行封存。使用者的封存信箱僅供該使用者使用。Microsoft 保留在使用者封存信箱中用來儲存其他使用者之封存資料的執行個體中拒絕不受限封存的權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p144">Using journaling, transport rules, or auto-forwarding rules to copy messages to an Exchange Online mailbox for the purposes of archiving is not permitted. A user's archive mailbox is intended for just that user. Microsoft reserves the right to deny unlimited archiving in instances where a user's archive mailbox is used to store archive data for other users.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1456">網站信箱<sup>4</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1456">Site mailboxes<sup>4</sup></span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1457">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1457">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1458">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1458">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1459">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1459">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1460">公用資料夾信箱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1460">Public folder mailboxes</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1461">50 GB<sup>5</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1461">50 GB<sup>5</sup></span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1462">100 GB<sup>5</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1462">100 GB<sup>5</sup></span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1463">100 GB<sup>5</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1463">100 GB<sup>5</sup></span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1464">群組信箱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1464">Group mailboxes</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1465">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1465">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1466">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1466">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1467">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1467">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
   
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1468"><sup>1</sup> 每位使用者初始會獲得 100 GB 的封存信箱儲存空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1468"><sup>1</sup> Each user initially receives 100 GB of storage in the archive mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1469">開啟自動展開封存時，當儲存容量達到 100 GB 時，會自動加入額外的儲存空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1469">When auto-expanding archiving is turned on, additional storage is automatically added when the 100 GB storage capacity is reached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1470">如需詳細資訊，請參閱在 Office 365 中的無限制封存概觀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1470">For more information, see Overview of unlimited archiving in Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1471">如需可用性的詳細資訊，請參閱 Office 365 藍圖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1471">See the Office 365 Roadmap for details about availability.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1472"> 
<sup>2</sup> 若要存取共用信箱，使用者必須擁有 Exchange Online 授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1472"> 
<sup>2</sup> To access a shared mailbox, a user must have an Exchange Online license.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1473">共用信箱不需要個別的授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1473">Shared mailboxes don't require a separate license.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1474">不過，如果您想要在共用信箱上啟用就地封存、就地保留或訴訟資料暫留，則需要 Exchange Online Plan 2 授權或 Exchange Online Plan 1 與 Exchange Online 封存授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1474">However, if you want to enable In-Place Archive or put an In-Place Hold or a Litigation Hold on a shared mailbox, then an Exchange Online Plan 2 license or an Exchange Online Plan 1 with Exchange Online Archiving license is required.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1475">如果您對共用信箱啟用就地封存與自動展開封存，當封存信箱達到 100 GB 的儲存容量時，會自動加入額外的儲存空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1475">If you enable In-Place Archive and auto-expanding archiving for a shared mailbox, additional storage is automatically added when the 100 GB storage capacity for the archive mailbox is reached.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1476"> 
<sup>3</sup> 資源信箱不需要授權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1476"> 
<sup>3</sup> Resource mailboxes don't require a license.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1477"> 
<sup>4</sup> 網站信箱的建立和管理是在 SharePoint Online 中進行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1477">Site mailboxes are created and managed in SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1478">如需詳細資訊，請參閱「為在 Office 365 中使用網站信箱作準備」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1478">For more information, see Prepare for using site mailboxes in Office 365.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1479"> 
<sup>5</sup> 您最多可以有 1,000 個公用資料夾信箱，而且所有公用資料夾信箱的大小總和上限為 50 TB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1479"> 
<sup>6</sup> You are limited to 1000 public folder mailboxes, and the maximum total size of all public folder mailboxes is 50 TB.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1480"> 
<sup>6</sup>「就地封存」僅可用來封存已套用授權之單一使用者或實體 (例如共用信箱) 的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1480">In-Place Archive can only be used to archive mail for a single user or entity (such as a shared mailbox) for which a license has been applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1481">禁止使用「就地封存」來儲存多個使用者或實體的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1481">Using an In-Place Archive as a means of storing mail from multiple users or entities is prohibited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1482">例如，IT 系統管理員不能建立共用信箱，再由使用者純粹為了封存的目的來複製它 (透過 [副本] 或 [密件副本] 欄位，或透過傳輸規則)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1482">For example, an IT administrator can't create a shared mailbox and have users copy it (through the Cc or Bcc field, or through a transport rule) for the explicit purpose of archiving.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1483">請注意，多人使用的共用信箱不會實際儲存個別使用者的電子郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1483">Note that a shared mailbox that multiple people use does not actually store email for those individual users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1484">多個使用者可以存取，且傳送電子郵件做為共用信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1484">Multiple users have access, and they send email as the shared mailbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1485">因此，只有傳送至共用信箱或從共用信箱寄出的電子郵件會儲存在共用信箱中，做為共用信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1485">Therefore, the only emails stored in the shared mailbox are those sent to or from it,  as  the shared mailbox.</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1486"> 
<sup>7</sup> 如果您已在 Exchange Online 中建立保留原則，則只有當使用者的主要信箱大於 10 MB 時，系統才會自動將郵件移到使用者的封存信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1486">9 If you have created a retention policy in Exchange Online, messages will be automatically moved to a user's archive mailbox only if the user's primary mailbox is larger than 10 MB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1487">若信箱小於 10 MB，則保留原則不會不該信箱自動執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1487">The retention policy will not run automatically for mailboxes that are smaller than 10 MB.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="capacity-alerts"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1488">容量警示</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1488">Capacity alerts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1489">Exchange Online 在使用者信箱接近容量上限或已達上限時提供三種通知類型：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1489">Exchange Online provides three kinds of notifications when a user's mailbox is nearing, or at, capacity:</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p150">**警告** 使用者收到信箱接近大小限制上限的電子郵件警告。此警告的目的是讓使用者刪除不需要的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p150">**Warning** The user receives an email warning that the mailbox is approaching the maximum size limit. This warning is intended to encourage users to delete unwanted mail.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p151">**禁止傳送** 當達到信箱大小限制時，使用者會收到禁止傳送通知電子郵件。在刪除足夠的電子郵件以將信箱容量降低至大小上限前，使用者無法傳送新的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p151">**Prohibit Send** The user receives a prohibit-send notification email when the mailbox size limit is reached. The user cannot send new messages until enough email is deleted to bring the mailbox below the size limit.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p152">**禁止傳送/接收** 當達到信箱大小上限時，Exchange Online 將拒絕任何來信，並將傳送未傳遞回報 (NDR) 給寄件者。寄件者可選擇稍後嘗試重新傳送該郵件。若再次收到訊息，使用者必須刪除電子郵件，直到信箱低於大小限制為止。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p152">**Prohibit Send/Receive** Exchange Online rejects any incoming mail when the mailbox size limit is reached, and sends a non-delivery report (NDR) to the sender. The sender has the option to try resending the mail later. To receive messages again, the user must delete email until the mailbox is below the size limit.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1497">**功能**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1497">**Feature**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1498">**Office 365 A1**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1498">**Office 365 A1**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1499">**Office 365 A3**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1499">**Office 365 A3**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1500">**Office 365 A5**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1500">**Office 365 A5**</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1501">警告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1501">Warning</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1502">49 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1502">49 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1503">98 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1503">98 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1504">98 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1504">98 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1505">禁止傳送</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1505">Prohibit Send</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1506">49.5 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1506">49.5 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1507">99 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1507">99 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1508">99 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1508">99 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1509">禁止傳送/接收</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1509">Prohibit Send/Receive</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1510">50 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1510">50 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1511">100 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1511">100 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1512">100 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1512">100 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
   
#### <a name="mailbox-folder-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1513">信箱資料夾限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1513">Mailbox folder limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p153">這些限制是為了讓信箱容量不超過 Exchange Online 可支援的已知大小範圍。這些限制的目的在於防止每一資料夾有無限多個信箱項目、每一信箱有無限多個資料夾，或每一 Exchange Online 組織有無限多個公用資料夾。為了實用目的，信箱資料夾限制實際上不受限，且足以支援大多數的 Exchange Online 信箱和已移轉至 Exchange Online 的內部部署信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p153">These limits are intended to limit mailboxes to known dimensions that can be supported in Exchange Online. The goal of these limits is to prevent an infinite number of mailbox items per folder, an infinite number of folders per mailbox, or an infinite number of public folders per Exchange Online organization. For practical purposes, mailbox folder limits are in effect unlimited and sufficient to support most Exchange Online mailboxes and on-premises mailboxes that are migrated to Exchange Online.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p154">**每一信箱資料夾的郵件數目上限** 指定信箱資料夾的郵件數目上限。達到此限制時，新郵件便無法傳遞或儲存至資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p154">**Maximum number of messages per mailbox folder** Specifies the maximum number of messages for a mailbox folder. New messages can't be delivered or saved in a folder when this limit is reached.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p155">**每一信箱資料夾的郵件數目警告** 指定在 Exchange Online 傳送警告訊息給信箱擁有者之前，信箱資料夾可以保留的郵件數目。達到此配額時，一天會傳送一次警告訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p155">**Warning for number of messages per mailbox folder** Specifies the number of messages that a mailbox folder can hold before Exchange Online sends a warning message to the mailbox owner. When this quota is reached, warning messages are sent once a day.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p156">**[可復原的項目] 資料夾中每一資料夾的郵件數目上限** 指定 [可復原的項目] 資料夾中每個資料夾可以包含的郵件數目上限。資料夾超過此限制時，就無法儲存新郵件。例如，如果 [可復原的項目] 資料夾中的 [刪除] 資料夾已超過郵件計數限制，而且信箱擁有者嘗試從其信箱中永久刪除項目，則刪除會失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p156">**Maximum number of messages per folder in the Recoverable Items folder** Specifies the maximum number of messages that can be contained in each folder in the Recoverable Items folder. When a folder exceeds this limit, it can't store new messages. For example, if the Deletions folder in the Recoverable Items folder has exceeded the message count limit and the mailbox owner attempts to permanently delete items from their mailbox, the deletion will fail.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1524">**[可復原的項目] 資料夾中每一資料夾的郵件數目警告** 指定在 Exchange Online 於應用程式事件記錄中記錄事件之前，[可復原的項目] 資料夾中每個資料夾可以保留的郵件數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1524">**Warning for number of messages per folder in the Recoverable Items folder** Specifies the number of messages that each folder in the Recoverable Items folder can hold before Exchange Online logs an event to the application event log.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p157">**每一信箱資料夾的子資料夾數目上限** 指定可以在信箱資料夾中建立的子資料夾數目上限。達到此限制時，信箱擁有者就無法建立新的子資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p157">**Maximum number of subfolders per mailbox folder** Specifies the maximum number of subfolders that can be created in a mailbox folder. The mailbox owner won't be able to create a new subfolder when this limit is reached.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p158">**每一信箱資料夾的子資料夾數目警告** 指定在 Exchange Online 傳送警告訊息給信箱擁有者之前，可以在信箱資料夾中建立的子資料夾數目。達到此配額時，一天會傳送一次警告訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p158">**Warning for number of subfolders per mailbox folder** Specifies the number of subfolders that can be created in a mailbox folder before Exchange Online sends a warning message to the mailbox owner. When this quota is reached, warning messages are sent once a day.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p159">**資料夾階層深度上限** 指定信箱的資料夾階層中的層級數目上限。達到此限制時，信箱擁有者就無法在信箱資料夾的資料夾階層中建立另一個層級。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p159">**Maximum folder hierarchy depth** Specifies the maximum number of levels in the folder hierarchy of a mailbox. The mailbox owner won't be able to create another level in the folder hierarchy of the mailbox folder when this limit is reached.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p160">**資料夾階層深度警告** 指定在 Exchange Online 傳送警告訊息給信箱擁有者之前，可以在信箱資料夾的資料夾階層中建立的層級數目。達到此配額時，一天會傳送一次警告訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p160">**Warning for folder hierarchy depth** Specifies the number of levels in the folder hierarchy of a mailbox folder that can be created before Exchange Online sends a warning message to the mailbox owner. When this quota is reached, warning messages are sent once a day.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p161">**最大公用資料夾數目** 指定完整公用資料夾階層中的最大公用資料夾數目。達到此限制時，必須先刪除現有公用資料夾，才能建立新的公用資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p161">**Maximum number of public folders** Specifies the maximum number of public folders in the complete public folder hierarchy. When this limit is reached, existing public folders must be deleted before new public folders can be created.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p162">**每一公用資料夾的子資料夾數目上限** 指定可在公用資料夾中建立的子資料夾數目上限。達到此限制時，即無法在公用資料夾中建立新的子資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p162">**Maximum number of subfolders per public folder** Specifies the maximum number of subfolders that can be created in a public folder. New subfolders can't be created in a public folder when this limit is reached.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p163">**每一公用資料夾的子資料夾數目警告** 指定在 Exchange Online 傳送警告訊息給資料夾擁有者之前，可以在公用資料夾中建立的子資料夾數目。如果沒有擁有者存在，則會傳送警告訊息給具有擁有者權限的使用者。達到此配額時，一天會傳送一次警告訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p163">**Warning for number of subfolders per public folder** Specifies the number of subfolders that can be created in a public folder before Exchange Online sends a warning message to the folder owner. If no owner exists, warning messages are sent to users with Owner permissions. When this quota is reached, warning messages are sent once a day.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1600">每一公用資料夾的子資料夾數目警告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1600">Warning for number of subfolders per public folder</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1601">9000</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1601">9000</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1602">9000</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1602">9000</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1603">9000</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1603">9000</span></span>  <br/> |
   
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1604"><sup>1</sup> 您可以在 Office 365 使用者之間 (郵件永遠不會離開 Office 365 資料中心) 傳送和接收最多 150 MB 的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1604">You can send and receive up to 150 MB messages between Office 365 users (where the message never leaves the Office 365 datacenters).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1605">Office 365 資料中心外路由傳送的郵件都會受限於額外 33% 轉譯編碼增加，如此一來，郵件大小上限是 112 MB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1605">Messages that are routed outside of the Office 365 datacenters are subject to an additional 33% translation encoding increase, in which case the maximum message size is 112 MB.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="message-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1606">郵件限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1606">Message limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p165">**郵件大小限制** 為避免大型郵件封鎖其他郵件的遞送，以及影響所有使用者的服務效能，需要設定郵件大小限制。這些限制包含附件，且適用於整個組織內的所有郵件 (內送、外寄和內部)。大於此上限的郵件將不會傳遞，而寄件者將收到未傳遞回報 (NDR)。雖然郵件大小上限無法上調、下調或依各使用者為基準設定，管理員仍可建立傳輸規則來限制任何個別附件的最高大小上限。若要深入了解，請參閱 [Office 365 現在可支援較大的電子郵件訊息](https://www.microsoft.com/zh-TW/microsoft-365/blog/2015/04/15/office-365-now-supports-larger-email-messages-up-to-150-mb/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p165">**Message size limit** Message size limits are necessary to prevent large messages from blocking delivery of other messages and affecting service performance for all users. These limits include attachments, and apply organization-wide to all messages (inbound, outbound, and internal). Messages larger than this limit will not be delivered, and the sender will receive a non-delivery report (NDR). While message size limits can be configured up, down, or on a per-user basis, administrators can also create transport rules to limit the maximum size of any individual attachment. To learn more, see [Office 365 now supports larger email messages](https://www.microsoft.com/zh-TW/microsoft-365/blog/2015/04/15/office-365-now-supports-larger-email-messages-up-to-150-mb/).</span></span>
    
   > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1612">部分電子郵件用戶端可擁有較低的郵件大小或可限制個別檔案附件的大小為小於 Exchange Online 郵件大小上限的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1612">Particular email clients may have lower message size limits or may limit the size of an individual file attachment to a value that is less than the Exchange Online message size limit.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1613">**主旨長度限制** 電子郵件主旨行中允許的文字字元數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1613">**Subject length limit** The maximum number of text characters allowed in the subject line of an email message.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p166">**檔案附件限制** 電子郵件中允許的檔案附件數目上限。即使所有檔案附件的大小總計沒有違反郵件大小限制，郵件中允許的附件數目仍然具有限制。此限制會由 Multipart 郵件限制控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p166">**File attachments limit** The maximum number of file attachments allowed in an email message. Even if the total size of all the file attachments doesn't violate the message size limit, there is still a limit on how many attachments are allowed in the message. This limit is controlled by the multipart message limit.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1617">**檔案附件大小限制** 單一附件的檔案大小上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1617">**File attachment size limit** The maximum file size of a single attachment.</span></span> 
    
    > [!NOTE] 
    > <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1618">這是單一附件的檔案大小上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1618">This is the maximum file size of a single attachment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1619">個別用戶端方案 (包括網頁版 Outlook) 可能會規定附件大小需低於此上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1619">Individual client programs, including Outlook Web App, may limit the size of attachments below this maximum.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1620">Exchange ActiveSync 未針對個別附件實作附件大小限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1620">Exchange ActiveSync does not implement attachment size limits on an individual attachment basis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1621">Exchange ActiveSync 郵件的所有附件大小總和必須小於郵件大小限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1621">The total size of all attachments to an Exchange ActiveSync message must be less than the message size limit.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p168">**Multipart 郵件限制** MIME Multipart 郵件中允許的郵件內文部分數目上限。此限制也會控制郵件允許的檔案附件數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p168">**Multipart message limit** The maximum number of message body parts that are allowed in a MIME multipart message. This limit also controls the maximum number of file attachments that are allowed in a message.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1624">**內嵌郵件深度限制** 電子郵件中允許的轉寄電子郵件數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1624">**Embedded message depth limit** The maximum number of forwarded email messages that are allowed in an email message.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1681"><sup>1</sup> Office 365 系統管理員可以指定 1 MB 到 150 MB 之間的自訂限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1681"><sup>1</sup> Office 365 Administrators can specify a custom limit between 1 MB and 150 MB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1682">不過，您可以傳送或接收的郵件大小也取決於您的電子郵件用戶端或解決方案支援的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1682">However, the size of message you can send or receive also depends on what your email client or solution supports.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1683">如需自訂您的組織允許的最大郵件大小的詳細資訊，請參閱 [Office 365 現在支援較大的電子郵件訊息](https://www.microsoft.com/zh-TW/microsoft-365/blog/2015/04/15/office-365-now-supports-larger-email-messages-up-to-150-mb/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1683">For more information about customizing the maximum allowed message size for your organization, see [Office 365 now supports larger email messages](https://www.microsoft.com/zh-TW/microsoft-365/blog/2015/04/15/office-365-now-supports-larger-email-messages-up-to-150-mb/).</span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1684"> 
<sup>2</sup> 您可以在 Office 365 使用者之間 (郵件永遠不會離開 Office 365 資料中心) 傳送和接收最多 150 MB 的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1684"> 
<sup>2</sup> You can send and receive up to 150 MB messages between Office 365 users (where the message never leaves the Office 365 datacenters).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1685">Office 365 資料中心外路由傳送的郵件都會受限於額外 33% 轉譯編碼增加，如此一來，郵件大小上限是 112 MB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1685">Messages that are routed outside of the Office 365 datacenters are subject to an additional 33% translation encoding increase, in which case the maximum message size is 112 MB.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1686"> 
<sup>3</sup> OWA 會計算您的訊息可能受限於編碼增加 33% 的可能性，並且會將您可以傳送的郵件大小限制為小於已配置的設定 25%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1686"> 
<sup>3</sup> OWA accounts for the possibility that your message may be subject to the 33% encoding increase and restricts the size of message you can send to 25% less than the configured setting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1687">例如，如果您自訂的設定是 100 MB 的郵件大小上限，您可以傳送的郵件不超過 75 MB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1687">For example, if you customize your settings for a 100 MB maximum message size, you can send messages no larger than 75 MB.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1688"> 
<sup>4</sup> Exchange Online 會計算要移動至 Exchange Online 的郵件大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1688"> 
<sup>4</sup> The size of messages to be moved into Exchange Online are computed by Exchange Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1689">Exchange Server 2013 之前的 Exchange 版本可能報告較小的項目大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1689">Versions of Exchange prior to Exchange Server 2013 may report a smaller item size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1690">此限制適用於使用任何支援的 Exchange 信箱複寫服務來移動基本遷移。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1690">This limit applies to move based migrations using any supported Exchange Mailbox Replication Service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1691">其他遷移方法 (轉換、分段、IMAP、PST) 和其他第三方工具都受限於一般訊息大小限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1691">Other migration methods (Cutover, Staged, IMAP, PST) and other third party tools are limited by the general message size limit.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1692"> 
<sup>5</sup> 如需 OME 與新功能的相關資訊，請參閱 [設定以 Azure 資訊保護為基礎所建置的全新 Office 365 郵件加密功能](https://support.office.com/article/Set-up-new-Office-365-Message-Encryption-capabilities-built-on-top-of-Azure-Information-Protection-7ff0c040-b25c-4378-9904-b1b50210d00e?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1692"> 
<sup>5</sup> For information about OME with new capabilities, see [Set up new Office 365 Message Encryption capabilities built on top of Azure Information Protection](https://support.office.com/article/Set-up-new-Office-365-Message-Encryption-capabilities-built-on-top-of-Azure-Information-Protection-7ff0c040-b25c-4378-9904-b1b50210d00e?ui=en-US&amp;rs=en-US&amp;ad=US).</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="receiving-and-sending-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1693">接收及傳送限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1693">Receiving and sending limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p173">接收及傳送限制會套用至郵件、寄件者或收件者，以便抵禦垃圾郵件和大量郵寄蠕蟲或病毒。這些限制有助於保護系統的健康情況，並確保使用者安全。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p173">Receiving and sending limits are applied to combat spam and mass-mailing worms or viruses. These limits help to protect the health of our systems and keep our users safe.</span></span>
  
#### <a name="receiving-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1696">接收限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1696">Receiving limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p174">接受限制會套用至使用者、群組或公用資料夾每小時能接收的訊息數量。這會同時套用至從網際網路和內部部署伺服器接收的訊息。當超過接收限制時，任何傳送到該信箱的電子郵件將會收到未傳遞報告，指出信箱已超過最大傳遞臨界值。一個小時之後，將會重新整理限制，而信箱就能夠再度接收郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p174">Receiving limits apply to the number of messages that a user, group, or public folder can receive per hour. This applies for both messages received from the Internet and from on-premises servers. When the receiving limit has been exceeded, any emails sent to that mailbox will receive a non-delivery report stating that the mailbox has exceeded the maximum delivery threshold. After one hour, the limit will refresh and the mailbox will once again be able to receive messages.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1701">**功能**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1701">**Feature**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1702">**Office 365 A1**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1702">**Office 365 A1**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1703">**Office 365 A3**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1703">**Office 365 A3**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1704">**Office 365 A5**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1704">**Office 365 A5**</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1705">已接收的訊息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1705">Messages received</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1706">每小時 3600 封訊息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1706">3600 messages per hour</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1707">每小時 3600 封訊息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1707">3600 messages per hour</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1708">每小時 3600 封訊息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1708">3600 messages per hour</span></span>  <br/> |
   
#### <a name="sending-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1709">傳送限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1709">Sending limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1710">傳送限制會套用至使用者可以從 Exchange Online 帳戶傳送的收件者數量、訊息數量和每封訊息的收件者數量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1710">Sending limits apply to the number of recipients, number of messages, and number of recipients per message that a user can send from their Exchange Online account.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p175">就儲存於組織通訊錄中的通訊群組而言，系統會將群組視為一位收件者。就儲存於信箱之 [連絡人] 資料夾中的通訊群組而言，則系統將群組中的成員視為個別收件者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p175">For distribution groups stored in an organization's address book, the group is counted as one recipient. For distribution groups stored in the Contacts folder of a mailbox, the members of the group are counted individually.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p176">**收件者流量限制** 為了減少來路不明的大量郵件遞送，Exchange Online 擁有防止使用者與應用程式傳送大量電子郵件的收件者限制。這些限制會套用至每位使用者的所有外寄和內部郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p176">**Recipient rate limit** To discourage the delivery of unsolicited bulk messages, Exchange Online has recipient limits that prevent users and applications from sending large volumes of email. These limits are applied per-user to all outbound and internal messages.</span></span> 
    
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1715">Exchange Online 客戶若需要傳送合法的大量商業電子郵件（例如客戶電子報），應使用專門提供這些服務的第三方供應商。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1715">Exchange Online customers who need to send legitimate bulk commercial email (for example, customer newsletters) should use third-party providers that specialize in these services.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1716">**收件者限制** 此為單封電子郵件中 [收件者:]、[副本:] 和 [密件副本:]欄位允許的收件者數量上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1716">**Recipient limit** This is the maximum number of recipients allowed in the To:, Cc:, and Bcc: fields for a single email message.</span></span> 
    
    > [!NOTE]
    > <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p177">基於收件者流量限制和收件者限制的用意，組織共用通訊錄中所儲存的通訊群組會算為一位收件者。在個人通訊群組清單中，每位收件者皆分開計算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p177">For the purposes of the recipient rate limit and the recipient limit, a distribution group that is stored in the organization's shared address book counts as one recipient. In a personal distribution list, each recipient is counted separately.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p178">**郵件流量限制**郵件流量限制會決定使用者在指定時間內從 Exchange Online帳戶傳送的郵件數量。此限制可協助防止單一寄件者的系統資源使用量過高。如果使用者提交郵件的速率超過透過 SMTP 用戶端提交的限制，則會拒絕郵件，用戶端必須重試。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p178">**Message rate limit** Message rate limits determine how many messages a user can send from their Exchange Online account within a specified period of time. This limit helps prevent overconsumption of system resources by a single sender. If a user submits messages at a rate that exceeds the limit via SMTP client submission, the messages will be rejected and the client will need to retry.</span></span>

#### <a name="reporting-and-message-trace-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1742">報告和郵件追蹤限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1742">Reporting and message trace limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1743">如需報告和郵件追蹤限制，請參閱 [Exchange Online Protection 的報告和郵件追蹤](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/SecurityCompliance/eop/reporting-and-message-trace-in-exchange-online-protection)中的「報告和郵件追蹤資料可用性和延遲」一節。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1743">For reporting and message trace limits, see the "Reporting and message trace data availability and latency" section in [Reporting and Message Trace in Exchange Online Protection](https://docs.microsoft.com/office365/SecurityCompliance/eop/reporting-and-message-trace-in-exchange-online-protection).</span></span>
  
#### <a name="retention-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1744">保留限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1744">Retention limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1745">這些限制會控制可存取 [收件匣] 內特定資料夾中項目的時間長度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1745">These limits control the length of time that items in specific folders in the Inbox can be accessed.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1746">**[刪除的郵件] 資料夾保留期間** 自動移除項目之前可保留在 [刪除的郵件] 資料夾中的天數上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1746">**Deleted Items folder retention period** The maximum number of days that items can remain in the Deleted Items folder before they're automatically removed.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1747">**從 [刪除的郵件] 資料夾移除之項目的保留期間** 從 [刪除的郵件] 資料夾移除的項目在被永久刪除之前可保留的天數上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1747">**Retention period for items removed from the Deleted Items folder** The maximum numbers of days that items removed from the Deleted Items folder are retained before they're permanently deleted.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1748">**[垃圾郵件] 資料夾保留期間** 自動移除項目之前可保留在 [垃圾郵件] 資料夾中的天數上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1748">**Junk Email folder retention period** The maximum number of days that items can remain in the Junk Email folder before they're automatically removed.</span></span>

#### <a name="distribution-group-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1767">通訊群組限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1767">Distribution group limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1768">這些限制會套用至組織共用通訊錄中的通訊群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1768">These limits apply to distribution groups in your organization's shared address book.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1769">**通訊群組成員人數上限** 收件者總數是在通訊群組擴充之後決定的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1769">**Maximum number of distribution group members** The total recipient count is determined after distribution group expansion.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p180">**傳送郵件給大型通訊群組的限制** 通訊群組如果包含這項限制所指定的成員人數，就必須設有傳遞管理或郵件核准選項。傳遞管理會指定一份寄件者清單，只有這些寄件者才能傳送郵件至此通訊群組。郵件核准會指定一位或多位仲裁者，郵件必須通過他們的核准才能傳送至此通訊群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p180">**Limit sending messages to large distribution groups** Distribution groups that contain the number of members specified by this limit must have delivery management or message approval options configured. Delivery management specifies a list of senders who are allowed to send messages to the distribution group. Message approval specifies one or more moderators who must approve all messages sent to the distribution group.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p181">**大型通訊群組的郵件大小上限** 如果郵件是要傳送給 5,000 位以上的收件者，則該郵件大小不可超過此限制。如果郵件大小超過限制，郵件不會傳遞出去，而且寄件者會收到未傳遞回報 (NDR)。收件者總數是在通訊群組擴充之後決定的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p181">**Maximum message size for large distribution groups** If a message is sent to 5,000 or more recipients, the message size can't exceed this limit. If the message size exceeds the limit, the message isn't delivered, and the sender receives a non-delivery report (NDR). The total recipient count is determined after distribution group expansion.</span></span>

#### <a name="journal-transport-and-inbox-rule-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1803">日誌、傳輸和收件匣規則限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1803">Journal, transport, and inbox rule limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p183">下列清單包括套用至日誌規則、傳輸規則 (也稱為組織規則) 的限制，以及套用至「收件匣」規則的限制。「收件匣」規則是由個別使用者所設定，並且套用至由個別使用者的信箱所傳送和接收的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p183">The following list includes limits that apply to journal rules, transport rules (also known as organization-wide rules), and limits that apply to Inbox rules. Inbox rules are set up by individual users and applied to messages sent and received by the individual user's mailbox.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1806">**規則數目上限** 組織中可以存在的日誌規則數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1806">**Maximum number of journal rules** The maximum number of journal rules that can exist in the organization.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1807">**傳輸規則數目上限** 組織中可以存在的規則數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1807">**Maximum number of transport rules** The maximum number of rules that can exist in the organization.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p184">**個別傳輸規則的大小上限** 單一傳輸規則中可以使用的字元數目上限。這些字元是用在條件、例外狀況和動作中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p184">**Maximum size of an individual transport rule** The maximum number of characters that can be used in a single transport rule. The characters are used in the conditions, exceptions, and actions.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p185">**所有傳輸規則中使用之所有規則運算式的字元限制** 在組織中的所有傳輸規則條件及例外狀況中，所有規則運算式所使用的字元總數。您可以有幾條規則使用又長又複雜的規則運算式，也可以有許多規則使用簡單的規則運算式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p185">**Character limit for all regular expressions used in all transport rules** The total number of characters used by all the regular expressions in all the transport rule conditions and exceptions in the organization. You can have a few rules that use long and complex regular expressions, or you can have many rules that use simple regular expressions.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1812">**附件內容的掃描限制** 傳輸規則條件可讓您檢查郵件附件的內容，但只會檢查從附件擷取的第 1 MB 文字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1812">**Scanning limits for attachment content** The transport rule conditions enable you to examine the content of message attachments, but only the first 1 MB of the text extracted from an attachment is inspected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1813">此 1 MB 限制是指從附件擷取的文字，而不是附件的檔案大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1813">This 1 MB limit refers to the text extracted from the attachment, not to the file size of the attachment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1814">例如，2 MB 檔案可能包含小於 1 MB 的文字，所以會檢查所有的文字</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1814">For example, a 2 MB file may contain less than 1 MB of text, so all of the text would be inspected</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p187">**所有傳輸規則新增到郵件的收件者人數上限** 當郵件由不同的傳輸規則進行處理時，可新增到郵件中的收件者人數是有限制的。達到此上限之後，就不再將任何其餘的收件者新增到郵件中。此外，傳輸規則也不能將通訊群組新增到郵件中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p187">**Maximum number of recipients added to a message by all transport rules** When a message is acted on by different transport rules, only a finite number of recipients can be added to the message. After the limit is reached, any remaining recipients aren't added to the message. Also, distribution groups can't be added to a message by a transport rule.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p188">**轉寄者限制** 可為收件匣或傳輸規則設定之具有重新導向動作的收件者人數上限。如果為某個規則設定的郵件重新導向收件者數目超過此數目，系統將不會套用該規則，而任何符合該規則條件的郵件將不會被重新導向到規則中所列的任何收件者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p188">**Forwardee limit** The maximum number of recipients that can be configured for an inbox or transport rule with a redirecting action. If a rule is configured to redirect a message to more than this number of recipients, the rule won't be applied and any message that satisfies the rule condition won't be redirected to any of the recipients listed in the rule.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p189">**重新導向郵件的次數** 根據收件匣規則自動重新導向、轉寄或回覆郵件的次數。例如，使用者 A 的收件匣規則會根據寄件者，將郵件重新導向到使用者 B。使用者 B 的收件匣規則會根據主旨行中的關鍵字，將郵件轉寄給使用者 C。如果某封郵件同時符合這兩項條件，該郵件將只會傳送給使用者 B 而不會轉寄給使用者 C，因為只允許重新導向一次。在此情況下，會捨棄郵件，而未將未傳遞回報 (NDR) 傳送給使用者 B，指出未將郵件傳遞給使用者 C。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p189">**Number of times a message is redirected** The number of times a message will be redirected, forwarded, or replied to automatically based on Inbox rules. For example, User A has an Inbox rule that redirects messages to User B, based on the sender. User B has an Inbox rule that forwards messages to User C based on keywords in the subject line. If a message satisfies both of these conditions, the message is only sent to User B; it's not forwarded to User C because only one redirection is allowed. In this case, the message is dropped without sending a non-delivery report (NDR) to User B indicating that the message wasn't delivered to User C.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1833">傳輸規則數目上限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1833">Maximum number of transport rules</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1834">300 條規則</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1834">300 rules</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1835">300 條規則</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1835">300 rules</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1836">300 條規則</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1836">300 rules</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1845">附件內容的掃描限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1845">Scanning limits for content of attachments</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1846">1 MB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1846">1 MB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1847">1 MB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1847">1 MB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1848">1 MB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1848">1 MB</span></span>  <br/> |

#### <a name="moderation-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1861">仲裁限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1861">Moderation limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1862">這些限制會控制在通訊群組和傳輸規則套用之郵件核准所採用的仲裁設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1862">These limits control the moderation settings that are used for message approval applied to distribution groups and transport rules.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1863">**仲裁信箱的大小上限** 如果仲裁信箱超過此限制，需要仲裁的郵件會就包含在傳回給寄件者的未傳遞回報 (NDR) 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1863">**Maximum size of the arbitration mailbox** If the arbitration mailbox exceeds this limit, messages that require moderation are returned to the sender in a non-delivery report (NDR).</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p190">**仲裁者人數上限** 可指派給單一仲裁通訊群組的仲裁者人數上限，或是可使用單一傳輸規則新增到郵件中的仲裁者人數上限。請注意，您無法將通訊群組指定為仲裁者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p190">**Maximum number of moderators** The maximum number of moderators that you can assign to a single moderated distribution group or that can be added to a message using a single transport rule. Note that you can't specify a distribution group as a moderator.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p191">**等候仲裁之郵件的到期日** 根據預設，等候仲裁的郵件會在兩天後過期。不過，過期的仲裁郵件處理會每七天執行一次，也就是說，仲裁郵件會在兩天到九天之間的任何時候過期。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p191">**Expiration for messages waiting for moderation** By default, a message waiting for moderation expires after two days. However, the processing of expired moderated messages runs every seven days. This means that a moderated message can expire at any time between two and nine days.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p192">**過期仲裁通知郵件的最大速率** 這項限制會設定過期仲裁郵件一小時內的通知郵件數目上限。這項限制是設置在資料中心內的每個信箱資料庫上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p192">**Maximum rate for expired moderation notification messages** This limit sets the maximum number of notification messages for expired moderated messages in a one-hour period. This limit is placed on each mailbox database in the datacenter.</span></span> 
    
    <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p193">在大量使用期間，某些寄件者可能不會收到有關仲裁郵件已過期的通知郵件。不過，這些通知還是可以使用傳遞回報找到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p193">During periods of heavy usage, some senders may not receive notification messages for moderated messages that have expired. However, these notifications are still discoverable using delivery reports.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1877">仲裁信箱的大小上限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1877">Maximum size of the arbitration mailbox</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1878">10 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1878">10 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1879">10 GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1879">10 GB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1880">10GB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1880">10 GB</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1881">仲裁者人數上限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1881">Maximum number of moderators</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1882">10 位仲裁者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1882">10 moderators</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1883">10 位仲裁者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1883">10 moderators</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1884">10 位仲裁者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1884">10 moderators</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1885">等候仲裁的郵件到期日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1885">Expiration for messages waiting for moderation</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1886">2 天</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1886">2 days</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1887">2 天</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1887">2 days</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1888">2 天</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1888">2 days</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1889">過期仲裁通知郵件的最大速率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1889">Maximum rate for expired moderation notification messages</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1890">每小時 300 個過期通知</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1890">300 expiration notifications per hour</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1891">每小時 300 個過期通知</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1891">300 expiration notifications per hour</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1892">每小時 300 個過期通知</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1892">300 expiration notifications per hour</span></span>  <br/> |
   
#### <a name="exchange-activesync-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1893">Exchange ActiveSync 限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1893">Exchange ActiveSync limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1894">下列限制適用於 Microsoft Exchange ActiveSync，這是一種用戶端通訊協定，可以同步處理行動裝置與 Exchange 之間的信箱資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1894">The following limits apply to Microsoft Exchange ActiveSync, a client protocol that synchronizes mailbox data between mobile devices and Exchange.</span></span> 
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1895">**Exchange ActiveSync 裝置限制**：每個信箱的 Exchange ActiveSync 裝置數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1895">**Exchange ActiveSync device limit** The maximum number of Exchange ActiveSync devices per mailbox.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1896">**Exchange ActiveSync 裝置刪除限制**：Exchange 系統管理員可以在一個月內刪除的 Exchange ActiveSync 裝置數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1896">**Exchange ActiveSync device deletion limit** The maximum number of Exchange ActiveSync devices that an Exchange administrator can delete in a single month.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1897">**Exchange ActiveSync 檔案附件限制**：Exchange ActiveSync 裝置可以傳送或接收的郵件檔案附件大小上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1897">**Exchange ActiveSync file attachment limit** The maximum size of a message file attachment that can be sent or received by an Exchange ActiveSync device.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1910">Exchange ActiveSync 檔案附件限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1910">Exchange ActiveSync file attachment limit</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1911">25 MB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1911">25 MB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1912">25 MB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1912">25 MB</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1913">25 MB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1913">25 MB</span></span>  <br/> |
   
## <a name="onedrive-for-business-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1914">商務用 OneDrive 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1914">OneDrive for Business features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1915">商務用 OneDrive (之前稱為 SkyDrive Pro) 是雲端中的個人連線儲存空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1915">OneDrive for Business (formerly SkyDrive Pro) is personal online storage space in the cloud.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1916">請使用它輕鬆並安全地跨多個裝置來儲存工作檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1916">Use it to store and protect your work files while accessing them across multiple devices with ease.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1917">視需要與公司同事共用您的檔案，以及使用網頁版 Office 即時編輯 Office 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1917">Share your files with business colleagues as needed and collaborate on Office documents together in real time with the latest Office desktop, web, and mobile apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1918">請使用商務用 OneDrive 同步應用程式，將檔案同步到本機電腦。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1918">Sync files to your local computer using the OneDrive for Business sync client.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1919">商務用 OneDrive 隨附於 SharePoint Online，也可以作為獨立方案購買。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1919">OneDrive for Business is included in SharePoint Online and can also be purchased as a standalone plan.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1920">商務用 OneDrive 獨立選項包括網頁版 Office。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1920">The OneDrive for Business standalone option includes Office Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1921">若要深入了解，請參閱[什麼是商務用 OneDrive？](https://support.office.com/article/187f90af-056f-47c0-9656-cc0ddca7fdc2?ocmsassetID=HA102822076)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1921">To learn more, see [What is OneDrive for Business?](https://support.office.com/article/187f90af-056f-47c0-9656-cc0ddca7fdc2?ocmsassetID=HA102822076).</span></span>
  
### <a name="system-requirements"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1922">系統需求</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1922">System Requirements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1923">商務用 OneDrive 同步處理用戶端的系統需求與 OneDrive 用戶端不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1923">The OneDrive for Business sync client has different system requirements than the OneDrive client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1924">若要深入了解，請參閱[如何安裝商務用 OneDrive 同步處理用戶端](https://support2.microsoft.com/kb/2903984)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1924">To learn more, see [How to install the OneDrive for Business sync client](https://support2.microsoft.com/kb/2903984).</span></span>
  
### <a name="onedrive-for-business-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1925">商務用 OneDrive 限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1925">OneDrive for Business</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1926">商務用 OneDrive 方案 1 提供每位使用者 1 TB 的儲存空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1926">OneDrive for Business Plan 1 provides 1 TB of storage space per user.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1927">針對至少五位訂閱使用者，下列符合資格的方案提供每位使用者無限的 OneDrive 儲存空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1927">The following qualifying plans provide unlimited OneDrive storage per user for subscriptions with at least five users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1928">Microsoft 最初會提供每位使用者 5 TB 的儲存空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1928">Microsoft will provide an initial 5 TB of storage space per user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1929">想要額外 OneDrive 儲存空間的客戶可以視需要與「Microsoft 支援服務」連絡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1929">Customers who want additional OneDrive storage can request it as needed by contacting Microsoft Support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1930">少於五位使用者的訂閱會收到每個使用者 1 TB 的儲存空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1930">Subscriptions with less than five users receive 1 TB of personal cloud storage per user.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1931">Office 365 A1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1931">Office 365 A1</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1932">Office 365 A3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1932">Office 365 A3</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1933">Office 365 A5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1933">Office 365 A5</span></span>
    
<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1934">您無法為特定的 OneDrive 使用者配置更多儲存空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1934">You cannot allocate more storage to a specific OneDrive user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1935">不過，您可以降低使用者所看到的儲存空間容量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1935">However, you can lower the amount of storage that a user sees.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1936">如果 Office 365 企業版 F1 使用者需要更多儲存空間，您將需要升級至 Office 365 企業版 E1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1936">If an Office 365 Enterprise F1 user needs more storage, then you'll need to upgrade to Office 365 Enterprise E1.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1937">如需不可新增至商務用 OneDrive 之檔案類型的詳細資訊，請參閱[不能加入到清單或組件庫中的檔案類型](https://support.office.com/article/30be234d-e551-4c2a-8de8-f8546ffbf5b3)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1937">For information about file types that you can't add to OneDrive for Business, see [Types of files that cannot be added to a list or library](https://support.office.com/article/30be234d-e551-4c2a-8de8-f8546ffbf5b3).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1938">SharePoint Online 中包含商務用 OneDrive。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1938">OneDrive for Business is included in SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-1939">若要了解 SharePoint Online 的其他限制，例如網站集合配額、檔案上傳限制和儲存限制，請參閱 [SharePoint Online 軟體界限及限制](../sharepoint-online-service-description/sharepoint-online-limits.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-1939">To learn about additional limitations in SharePoint Online, such as site collection quotas, file upload limits, and storage limits, see [SharePoint Online software boundaries and limits](../sharepoint-online-service-description/sharepoint-online-limits.md).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-2881"><sup>1</sup> 若要使用資料夾同步處理，您必須擁有 Office 2013 或更新版本 (標準版或專業版)，或是包含 Office 應用程式的 Office 365 訂閱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-2881"><sup>1</sup> To use folder sync, you must have Office 2013 or later (Standard or Professional edition) or an Office 365 subscription that includes Office applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-2882">Office 365 商務基本版、Office 365 Enterprise E1 以及 Office 365 教育版方案並未包含 Office 桌面應用程式訂閱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-2882">Office 365 Business Essentials, Office 365 Enterprise E1, and Office 365 Education plans do not include subscriptions to Office desktop applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-2883">不過，如果您已安裝 Office 2013 或更新版本，並訂閱上述其中一個方案，就可以使用資料夾同步處理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-2883">However, you can use folder sync if you have Office 2013 or later installed and subscribe to one of these plans.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-2884"> 
<sup>2</sup> 因為 Kiosk 使用者不能是系統管理員，所以有 Kiosk 使用者的租用戶至少必須有一個企業使用者使用者，才能存取系統管理中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-2884">

<sup>8</sup> Sharing a document, library, or site by email with someone outside of your organization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-2889">系統管理員還是能夠將它開啟，但會出現警告訊息，指出它可能在您的國家/地區外進行檔案共用存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-2889">Administrators do have the ability to turn it on, but will get a warning message indicating that it could make files shared accessible outside of your country.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-2890">嘗試與組織外部的其他人共用的使用者會收到相同的警告訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-2890">Users who attempt to share with someone outside of the organization will receive the same warning message.</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-2891">

### <a name="skype-for-business-online-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-3454">商務用 Skype Online 限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-3454">Skype for Business Online Limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-3455">商務用 Skype Online 中的限制可分為下列類別：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-3455">[] The limits in Skype for Business Online fall into the following categories:</span></span>
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-3456">對等限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-3456">Peer-to-peer limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#peer-to-peer-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-3457">會議限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-3457">Meeting limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#meeting-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-3458">會議保留限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-3458">Meeting retention limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#meeting-retention-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="9adf7-3459">分鐘限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-3459">Minute limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#minute-limits)
    
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p219">適用於 Office 365 組織的限制可能會因為組織在服務中註冊的時間長短而有所不同。如果在 Microsoft 資料中心內變更了某項限制，可能需要一些時間才能將變更套用至所有現有的客戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p219">The limits applied to an Office 365 organization can differ depending on how long the organization has been enrolled in the service. When a limit is changed in the Microsoft data centers, it can take some time to apply the change to all existing customers.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="peer-to-peer-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9adf7-3462">對等限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-3462">Peer-to-peer limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-p220">**檔案傳輸限制**商務用 Skype Online IM 交談中可傳輸的檔案大小上限。若要了解哪些檔案類型不能進行檔案傳輸，請參閱有關[在商務用 Skype Online 中傳送和接收檔案或附件](https://docs.microsoft.com/SkypeForBusiness/troubleshoot/online-attachments/cant-send-receive-files-attachments)的 Microsoft 支援文章。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-p220">**File transfer limit** The maximum size of a file that can be transferred in a Skype for Business Online IM conversation. To learn which file types are blocked for file transfer, see the Microsoft Support article about [sending and receiving files or attachments in Skype for Business Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/SkypeForBusiness/troubleshoot/online-attachments/cant-send-receive-files-attachments).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9adf7-3465">**開啟的分頁交談限制** 商務用 Skype 使用者可同時開啟的交談索引標籤數目上限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9adf7-3465">**Open tabbed conversations limit** The maximum number of conversation tabs that a Skype for Business user can have open at one time.</span></span>
